## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|

| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |

| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Firefox Layout Engine Reflow Pipeline

I identified the key C++ source files implementing the three main components:

### 1. Frame Construction
- **`layout/base/nsCSSFrameConstructor.cpp/.h`** — The central frame construction class that creates/recreates frames when styles change or DOM nodes are inserted. Implements `ConstructBlock()`, `CreateIBSiblings()`, etc.
- **`layout/base/nsFrameManager.cpp/.h`** — Manages the frame tree structure.

### 2. Block Layout Reflow
- **`layout/generic/nsBlockFrame.cpp/.h`** — Core block layout frame with `Reflow()` driving block formatting context layout
- **`layout/generic/BlockReflowState.cpp/.h`** — Carries state across block reflow (float manager, line placement)
- **`layout/generic/nsBlockReflowContext.cpp/.h`** — Handles reflowing individual block children via `ReflowBlock()`
- **`layout/generic/ReflowInput.cpp/.h`** — Computes all input parameters for a reflow pass
- **`layout/generic/ReflowOutput.cpp/.h`** — Carries reflow output (desired size, overflow)
- **`layout/generic/nsLineLayout.cpp/.h`** — Inline/line layout within block frames
- **`layout/generic/nsLineBox.cpp/.h`** — Represents a line of inline content
- **`layout/generic/nsFloatManager.cpp/.h`** — Float placement management
- **`layout/generic/nsContainerFrame.cpp/.h`** — Base container frame with `ReflowChild()`
- **`layout/generic/AbsoluteContainingBlock.cpp/.h`** — Absolutely positioned children reflow

### 3. Dirty-Frame Invalidation
- **`layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp/.h`** — `ProcessRestyledFrames()` processes style changes and calls `FrameNeedsReflow()`
- **`layout/style/nsStyleChangeList.cpp/.h`** — Accumulates style change hints
- **`layout/style/nsChangeHin
